 ek varisht adhikari kaa kahana he, 'is prastaav main ensitisi ke tahat vibhinn sroton se milane vaali khufia soochnaaon ko ek jagah ekatra karne, in par jaanch karne or karrwai karne kii samoochee prakriya ko samahit karne kii baat shaamil hogi
 According to him, the proposed NCTC will be included directly under the Ministry of Home Affairs
 pichley prastaav main ise khufia beuro yani ibi ke antargat gathit karne kaa prastaav shaamil tha

 After Chidambaram, in 2013, the then Home Minister Sushil Kumar Shinde had also tried to reach a consensus among the states on the proposal for formation of NCTC but the success could not be achieved

 vaise chidambaram ke baad saal 2013 main tatkaaleen grih mantri susheel kumaar scindia ne bhi ensitisi ke gathan ke prastaav par rajyon ke bich sahmati kaayam karne kii koshish kii thi lekin kamyaabi nahin mil saki
 The Supreme Court has made stern remarks about the appointment to the Election Commission on Wednesday
 court ne kaha ki chunaav ayog main niyukti ke liye agar koi kanoon nahin he to court isamen dakhal degaa
 The court said in its remarks that so far all the appointments have been done fairly and correctly but we feel that there is no set procedure for this
 chunaav ayog main niyukti ke liye supreme court main ek yachika daayar kii gai thi, jisamen chunaav ayuktaon kii niyukti ke liye netaa vipaksh or mukhya nyaayadhish kii sadsyta vaale ek sanvaidhanik panel ke gathan kii maang kii gai thi
 During whose hearing, the court has given strict instructions to the Central Government that the Attorney General has asked whether the appointment can be done through secret ballot

 Hariyali Teej is celebrated on Tritiya Tithi of Shukla Paksha of the month of Sawan
 uttar bharat kii striyon kaa yah priy parv keval ek dharmik tyohaar nahin balki prakruti kaa utsav manaane kaa bhi din he
 This festival is also known as Shravani Teej or Kajri Teej
 is saal yah buudhvaar ko yani 26 july ko pad rahi he
 In this rainy season, the forest groves, fields etc
 are wrapped with a sheet of greenery
 sampurna prakruti hare rang ke manoram drishy se man ko trupt karti he
 Therefore, this festival of Sawan month is called Hariyali Teej
 puranic anushrutiyon ke anusaar, devi parvati ne mahadev shiv ko praapt karne ke liye sau varshon tak kathin tapasya kii thi
 He received Lord Shiva on this day by his tireless practice
 yahi kaaran he ki vivaahit mahilaayein apane sukhmay vivaahit jivan or akhand saubhaahgya kii prapti liye yah vrath rakhti hai
 According to tradition, virgin girls also keep this fast to get a worthy bride
 hariyaali teej ke is parv main menhadi, jhula or suhaag-chihn singhare kaa vishesh mahatv he
 Women decorate their hands with henna, a symbol of honey
 gaanv-kasbon main jagah-jagah jhule lagaae jate hai
 The women sing the Kajari song, swinging collectively
 is vishesh avasar par navvivaahitaaon ko unke sasuraal se maayke bulaane kii parampara he
 She brings Singhara with her
 saath hi sasuraal se kapade, gahane, suhaag kaa saamaan, mithai or menhadi bheji jaati he, jise teej kaa bhent mana jaataa he
 The comments anek sthanon par bade dhoomdhaam se mata parvati kii sawari nikaali jaati he or bhavy meley kaa aayojan hota he
 The Teej Mata Utsav held in Jaipur at such fairs is special
 yahaan devi parvati kii pratimaa, jinhen teej mata kaha jaataa he, kii puja raja-rajavaadon ke samay se hoti aa rahi he
 Devotees come from far and wide to get a glimpse of Teej Mata Parvati in Teej procession of Jaipur
 barish ke is mausam main van-upavan, khet aadi hariyaali kii chadar se lipte hote hai
 The entire nature satisfies the mind with a panoramic view of green
 isliye sawan maheene kaa yah tyohaar hariyaali teej kehalaata he
 According to mythological rituals, Goddess Parvati had undergone hard penance for a hundred years to attain Mahadev Shiva
 apni athak sadhana se unhone isi din bhagwaan shiv ko praapt kiya tha
 This is the reason why married women keep this fast in order to achieve their happy married life and unbroken good fortune
 parampara ke anusaar yogya var kii prapti ke liye kunvaari kanyaayein bhi yah vrath rakhti hai
 Henna, Jhula and Suhaag-mark Singhare have special importance in this festival of Hariyali Teej
 striyaan menhadi, jo ki suhaag kaa pratik he, se haathon ko sajaati hai
 Swings are carried out from place to place in villages and towns
 kajri geet gaati hui mahilaayein samuhik rup se jhula jhulati hai
 On this special occasion, there is a tradition of inviting newlyweds from their in-laws
 ve apane saath singhara laati he
 Also the in-laws are sent clothes, jewelry, suhaag items, sweets and henna, which is considered as Teej's offering
 tippaniyan Mata Parvati rides are taken out in many places with great pomp and grand fair is organized
 aise melon main jaipur main yojit hone vaala teej mata utsav vishesh darshneey he
 Here the idol of Goddess Parvati, called Teej Mata, has been worshiped since the time of the raja-rajvadas
 jaipur ke teej juluus main teej mata parvati kii ek jhalak paane or darshan ke liye dur-dur se shraddhalu aate hai

 kiran kumaar reddy ke saath baithak main faisla liya

 unhone rajya kii sadakon va rashtriya rajyamargon ko avaruddh kiya, jisase karnataka, tamilnadu or odisha se avaagaman avaruddh ho gaya

 Police used tear gas to disperse the mob that attacked the camp office of Congress state president Botsa Satyanarayana in Vizianagaram

 adhikariyon ne kaha he ki isse kuch jilon main vidyut aapurti par bura prabhaav padegaa

 yahaan telugu desham party or wiesar congress ke kaaryakartaaon main bhidnt ho gai

 In this, panellists from the party on TV channels in different states also participated
 amit shah ne kaha ki modi kii aguwai main centre sarkaar janata ke hit main acha kaam kar rahi he
 He said that it is the responsibility of the party spokespersons to take these works to the public and explain them in an easy manner
 shah ne sabhi pravaktaaon ko kaha ki teen saal main sarkaar ne bahut kaam kiya he
 Recently a major step has been taken regarding GST
 iske bare main logon ko bataanaa bhi party pravaktaaon kii zimmedaari he
 Shah said that the Modi government has started many schemes whose direct benefits are reaching the public
 unhone ujwala yojana, mudra yojana, jan dhan yojana, svachh bharat abhiyaan, gramin vikaas se sambandhit yojanaayen or yuvaaon ke rojgaar sambandhi yojanaon kaa prachaar karne ko kaha
 Shah said that by taking concrete steps to fill the pit on the development and economic front during the Congress government, not only the Modi government has filled it but also has erected the tower of development there
 gauratlab he ki bijepi 27 may se 15 june tak puure desh main modi sarkaar ke 3 saal kii uplabdhiyon kaa utsav manaayegi
 During this period, emphasis was also laid on better coordination for the visits of all the Union Ministers and Chief Ministers in the states, especially in non-bjp ruled states
 shah ne kaha ki modi sarkaar ne kai yojanaayen shuru kii hai jinka sidhaa laabh janata tak pahunch rahaa he
 He asked to promote Ujjwala Yojana, Mudra Yojana, Jan Dhan Yojana, Swachh Bharat Abhiyan, Rural Development Schemes and employment related schemes of youth
 shah ne kaha ki congress sarkaar ke dauraan vikaas or aarthik morche par jo gadde the, usko thos kadam uthaakar na sirf modi sarkaar ne bharaa balki vahaan vikaas kii minar khadi kii he
 Significantly, from May 27 to June 15, the BJP will celebrate 3 years of achievements of the Modi government across the country
 is dauraan rajyon khaastaur par gaiyr-bijepi shasit rajyon main tamaam kendriya mantriyon or mukhyamantriyon ke daure ko lekar behatar samanvay sthapit karne par bhi jor diya gaya

 ' In order to use the gold held with families and various institutions, the government has introduced a scheme under which a person or institution can deposit gold in banks and get interest
 dishanirdesh praaroop ke mutabik, kam se kam 30 gram sona jamaa karaya ja sakegaa or is par milane vaale byaaj par iskar yaa puunjigat laabh kar bhi nahin lagegaa
 According to this draft, if an individual or institution has excess gold, it can open a Gold Savings Account 'gold Saving Account' in banks for a period of at least one year by evaluating it from BIS certified hallmarking centers and as interest
 But you can get a cash or gold unit
 vitt mantralay ne is swarna maudrikaran yojana par sambhddha pakshon se do june tak tippaniyan dene ko kaha he
 India is the largest gold consuming country in the world and 800-1,000 tonnes of gold are imported here every year
 bharat main 20,000 ton sone kaa bhandar he, jiskaa na to vyapaar hota he na hi iskaa maudrikaran hota he
 The goal of this scheme is to collect idle gold with families and institutions so that the gems and jewelery sector can be taken forward and in the coming years, the dependence on imports to meet domestic demand can be reduced
 prastaavit yojana ke tahat bank graahakon ko swarna bachat khaataa khulne ke 30-60 din ke baad byaaj denge
 The draft guideline states that it is proposed to leave the decision on interest rate to the banks
 sona jamaa karne vaale ko adaa kiye jane vaale mooldhan or byaaj kaa hisaab kitaab sone main hi kiya jayega
 The draft stated that if a customer deposits 100 grams of gold and gets one percent interest, then on maturity, he will have 101 grams of gold in his account
 paripakvata ke maamle main dishanirdesh main kaha gaya he ki graahak ise nakad raashi main yaa sone ke rup main le saktaa he
 However, it has to be told while depositing gold
 yojana ke tahat jamaa avadhi kam se kam ek saal hogi or uske baad isi gunak main rakhi jaaegi
 The comments bainkon ko protsaahan dene ke liye isamen prastaav he ki bank jamaa kiye gaye sone ko siaraar athwa esaelaar ke badale rigerv bank ke paas rakh sakate hen
 However, this issue is still under investigation
 dishanirdesh ke mutabik bank videshi mudra hasil karne ke liye sone kii bikri bhi kar sakate hai
 Foreign currency thus acquired can be loaned to exporters and importers

 Addressing the rally, PM Modi said that during the time of our government, there was a terrorist attack on the army in Uri, after which you all have seen what has happened
 aapako bataa den ki uri aatanki hamale ke baad bharat ne pakistan adhikrut kashmir main ghuskar sargical strike kii thi or aatankiyon ke thikaanon ko tabah kar diya tha
 a large number of terrorists were also killed in it
 is karrwai ke baad bhi pakistan apni harakat se baj nahin aayaa or pulavama main aatanki hamalaa kiya gaya, jisamen siarpief ke 40 jawan shahid ho gaye
 After this incident, India entered into Pakistan and carried out an air strike and destroyed the bases of terrorist organization jaish-e-mohammed
 bhartiya sena kii is bahaduree ko sabhi ne dekha he
 PM Modi said, 'I salute all the brave soldiers who have lived in the service of the country
 inaki satarkta ke chalate hamaara desh surakshit he
 On this occasion, PM Modi flagged off the fastest train, Tejas
 yah train madurai se chennai ke bich daudegi
 Along with this, the foundation of the railway line between Rameswaram to Dhanushkodi was also laid
 railway line kii neenv rakhte hue piem modi ne kaha ki yah railway line 1964 ke aapadaa ke baad kshatigrast ho gai thi
 Despite the passage of time, little attention was paid to fixing it
 unhone kaha ki piem kisaan yojana ke tahat ek karod 10 lakh kisaanon ke khate main pehali instollment bheji ja chuki he
 Addressing the people, he said that just think that the scheme announced on February 1 was implemented in the same month
 hamane is yojana ko 24 din main lagu karne ke liye bina ruke 24 ghante kaam kiya
 PM Modi said that for the first time in 2014 after 30 years, a party formed the government with a majority
 iske jariye logon ne saaf massej diya ki wo aisi majboot sarkaar chaahate hai, jo kade faisle le sake
 The PM said that people want honesty, not dynasty
 log vikaas chaahate hai, vinaash nahin
 People want progress, not policy paralysis
 log avasar chaahate hai, avrodh nahin
 People want security, not deadlock
 log samekit growth chaahate hai, vot bank kii raajnneeti nahin
 During this time, PM Modi also talked about increasing the income of Indian fishermen
 unhone kaha ki agar ham machuaare bhai or bahanon kii inakam main badhottaree karnaa chaahate hai, to hamen matsay paalan se jude buniyadi dhaanche kaa vikaas karnaa hoga
 He said that the Government of India is sensitive to the safety and well-being of fishermen
 rajanyik prayaason se may 2014 se ab tak saikadon machuaaron ko srilanka se chhudvaaya gaya he
 Apart from this, PM Modi also addressed a rally in Visakhapatnam, Andhra Pradesh
 is dauraan unhone soobe ke mukhyamantri chandrababu naidu par hamalaa bolaa
 Without naming Naidu, Modi said that if the leaders here would have done their work honestly, they would not have to expose their failure to Modi
 is dauraan unhone kaha ki kuch logon ke saamne apana raajnneetik vajood bachaane kii chunauti he, jiske liye wo din-raat jhooth bol rahe hai
 a heartbreaking incident has come to light in Sangam Vihar
 50 saal ke ek sanakee shaks ne pados kii paanch bacchiyon ko jalaane kii koshish kii
 In time, the police rescued the five girls with the help of nearby people
 khabar ke mutabik aaropee bharat bhushan ne kanya pujan ke bahaane pados kii paanch bacchiyon ko apane ghar bulaayaa
 He fed the girls first, but when the girls talked about going home, he closed the door and cut the gas pipe
 iske baad usne ladakiyon or farsh par mitti kaa tel daal diya
 By then the parents of the children had reached outside the house of Bharat Bhushan, looking for them
 bharat bhushan ne haath main maachis lekar dhamkee deni shuru kar di ki wo paanchon bacchiyon ko jala degaa
 People called the police and informed them
 maukey par pahunchi police ne use samajhane kii koshish kii
 Arrangements were made to pour water into the room during a period of precaution
 padosiyon ne pani kii motor chalaa lee or ghar ke baahar geele chadar rakh diye gaye taaki aag lagane par in chaadaron ko bacchon par daalaa ja sake
 After this, the police opened the door with a big stone and the five girls were taken out safely
 bataaya jaataa he ki bharat bhushan kii bahu ne uske parivaar ke khilaaf dahej kaa cese darj karaayaa tha
 In this connection, some people of his family have also been arrested
 isi baat se naaraaz bharat bhushan par bacchiyon ko jalaane kii sanak savaar ho gai
 He says that these girls will also become daughters-in-law and ruin someone's house
 isliye wo in bacchiyon ko jalaakar maar dena chahta tha
